<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="be-explicit-with-your-instructions"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

  relative

  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none

  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Be explicit with your instructions</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.x models respond well to clear, explicit instructions. Being specific about your desired output can help enhance results. Customers who desire the &quot;above and beyond&quot; behavior from previous Claude models might need to more explicitly request these behaviors with newer models.</p>

<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="add-context-to-improve-performance"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative

  select-none

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Add context to improve performance</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Providing context or motivation behind your instructions, such as explaining to Claude why such behavior is important, can help Claude 4.x models better understand your goals and deliver more targeted responses.</p>
<div data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden border border-border-300 rounded-lg my-6"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="flex"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_48uinpfdaiv6brkljb_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_8uinpfdaiv6brkljb_" class="group w-full flex items-center gap-2 p-4 text-left transparent hover:bg-bg-300 focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-accent-secondary-100 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="text-text-500 transition-transform duration-200 flex-shrink-0 group-data-[state=&#x27;open&#x27;]:rotate-90" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M181.66,133.66l-80,80a8,8,0,0,1-11.32-11.32L164.69,128,90.34,53.66a8,8,0,0,1,11.32-11.32l80,80A8,8,0,0,1,181.66,133.66Z"></path></svg><span class="font-semibold text-text-100 flex-1 font-ui">Example: Formatting preferences</span></button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_48uinpfdaiv6brkljb_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="accordion-example:-formatting-preferences" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude is smart enough to generalize from the explanation.</p>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="be-vigilant-with-examples-and-details"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Be vigilant with examples &amp; details</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.x models pay close attention to details and examples as part of their precise instruction following capabilities. Ensure that your examples align with the behaviors you want to encourage and minimize behaviors you want to avoid.</p>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="long-horizon-reasoning-and-state-tracking"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Long-horizon reasoning and state tracking</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.5 models excel at long-horizon reasoning tasks with exceptional state tracking capabilities. It maintains orientation across extended sessions by focusing on incremental progressâ€”making steady advances on a few things at a time rather than attempting everything at once. This capability especially emerges over multiple context windows or task iterations, where Claude can work on a complex task, save the state, and continue with a fresh context window.</p>
<h4 class="text-lg font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="context-awareness-and-multi-window-workflows"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Context awareness and multi-window workflows</div></div></h4>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.5 models feature <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/context-windows#context-awareness-in-claude-sonnet-4-5">context awareness</a>, enabling the model to track its remaining context window (i.e. &quot;token budget&quot;) throughout a conversation. This enables Claude to execute tasks and manage context more effectively by understanding how much space it has to work.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Managing context limits:</strong></p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">If you are using Claude in an agent harness that compacts context or allows saving context to external files (like in Claude Code), we suggest adding this information to your prompt so Claude can behave accordingly. Otherwise, Claude may sometimes naturally try to wrap up work as it approaches the context limit. Below is an example prompt:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center justify-center"><div class="flex items-center justify-center transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12.5 3C13.3284 3 14 3.67157 14 13.3284 14 12.5 14H7V15.5C7 15.7761 7.22386 16 7.5 16H15.5C15.7761 16 16 15.7761 16 15.5V7.5C16 7.22386 15.7761 7 15.5 7H14V12.5ZM4.5 4C4.22386 4 4 4.22386 4 4.5V12.5C4 12.7761 4.22386 13 4.5 13H12.5C12.7761 13 13 12.7761 13 12.5V4.5C13 4.22386 12.7761 4 12.5 4H4.5Z"></path></svg></div><div class="flex items-center justify-center absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>Your context window will be automatically compacted as it approaches its limit, allowing you to continue working indefinitely from where you left off. Therefore, do not stop tasks early due to token budget concerns. As you approach your token budget limit, save your current progress and state to memory before the context window refreshes. Always be as persistent and autonomous as possible and complete tasks fully, even if the end of your budget is approaching. Never artificially stop any task early regardless of the context remaining.</code></pre></div></div>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">The <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agents-and-tools/tool-use/memory-tool">memory tool</a> pairs naturally with context awareness for seamless context transitions.</p>
<h4 class="text-lg font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="multi-context-window-workflows"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Multi-context window workflows</div></div></h4>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For tasks spanning multiple context windows:</p>
<ol class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item]">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Use a different prompt for the very first context window</strong>: Use the first context window to set up a framework (write tests, create setup scripts), then use future context windows to iterate on a todo-list.</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Have the model write tests in a structured format</strong>: Ask Claude to create tests before starting work and keep track of them in a structured format (e.g., <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">tests.json</code>). This leads to better long-term ability to iterate. Remind Claude of the importance of tests: &quot;It is unacceptable to remove or edit tests because this could lead to missing or buggy functionality.&quot;</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Set up quality of life tools</strong>: Encourage Claude to create setup scripts (e.g., <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">init.sh</code>) to gracefully start servers, run test suites, and linters. This prevents repeated work when continuing from a fresh context window.</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Starting fresh vs compacting</strong>: When a context window is cleared, consider starting with a brand new context window rather than using compaction. Claude 4.5 models are extremely effective at discovering state from the local filesystem. In some cases, you may want to take advantage of this over compaction. Be prescriptive about how it should start:</p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">&quot;Call pwd; you can only read and write files in this directory.&quot;</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">&quot;Review progress.txt, tests.json, and the git logs.&quot;</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">&quot;Manually run through a fundamental integration test before moving on to implementing new features.&quot;</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Provide verification tools</strong>: As the length of autonomous tasks grows, Claude needs to verify correctness without continuous human feedback. Tools like Playwright MCP server or computer use capabilities for testing UIs are helpful.</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Encourage complete usage of context</strong>: Prompt Claude to efficiently complete components before moving on:</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center justify-center"><div class="flex items-center justify-center transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" 13.3284 14 12.5 14H7V15.5C7 15.7761 7.22386 16 7.5 16H15.5C15.7761 16 16 15.7761 16 15.5V7.5C16 7.22386 15.7761 7 15.5 7H14V12.5ZM4.5 4C4.22386 4 4 4.22386 4 4.5V12.5C4 12.7761 4.22386 13 4.5 opacity-0" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>This is a very long task, so it may be beneficial to plan out your work clearly. It&#x27;s encouraged to spend your entire output context working on the task - just make sure you don&#x27;t run out of context with significant uncommitted work. Continue working systematically until you have completed this task.</code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="text-lg font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="state-management-best-practices"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>State management best practices</div></div></h4>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use structured formats for state data</strong>: When tracking structured information (like test results or task status), use JSON or other structured formats to help Claude understand schema requirements</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use unstructured text for progress notes</strong>: Freeform progress notes work well for tracking general progress and context</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use git for state tracking</strong>: Git provides a log of what&#x27;s been done and checkpoints that can be restored. Claude 4.5 models perform especially well in using git to track state across multiple sessions.</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Emphasize incremental progress</strong>: Explicitly ask Claude to keep track of its progress and focus on incremental work</li>
</ul>
<div data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden border border-border-300 rounded-lg my-6"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="flex"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_4quinpfdaiv6brkljb_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_quinpfdaiv6brkljb_" class="group w-full flex items-center gap-2 p-4 text-left transparent hover:bg-bg-300 focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-accent-secondary-100 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="text-text-500 transition-transform duration-200 flex-shrink-0 group-data-[state=&#x27;open&#x27;]:rotate-90" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M181.66,133.66l-80,80a8,8,0,0,1-11.32-11.32L164.69,128,90.34,53.66a8,8,0,0,1,11.32-11.32l80,80A8,8,0,0,1,181.66,133.66Z"></path></svg><span class="font-semibold text-text-100 flex-1 font-ui">Example: State tracking</span></button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_4quinpfdaiv6brkljb_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="accordion-example:-state-tracking" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="communication-style"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Communication style</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.5 models have a more concise and natural communication style compared to previous models:</p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">More direct and grounded</strong>: Provides fact-based progress reports rather than self-celebratory updates</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">More conversational</strong>: Slightly more fluent and colloquial, less machine-like</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Less verbose</strong>: May skip detailed summaries for efficiency unless prompted otherwise</li>
</ul>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">This communication style accurately reflects what has been accomplished without unnecessary elaboration.</p>
<h2 class="font-heading leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="guidance-for-specific-situations"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent

          font-base

          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Guidance for specific situations</div></div></h2>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="balance-verbosity"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Balance verbosity</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.5 models tend toward efficiency and may skip verbal summaries after tool calls, jumping directly to the next action. While this creates a streamlined workflow, you may prefer more visibility into its reasoning process.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">If you want Claude to provide updates as it works:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center justify-center"><div class="flex items-center justify-center transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" the work you&#x27;ve done.</code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="tool-usage-patterns"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

  justify-center

  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.5 models are trained for precise instruction following and benefits from explicit direction to use specific tools. If you say &quot;can you suggest some changes,&quot; it will sometimes provide suggestions rather than implementing themâ€”even if making changes might be what you intended.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For Claude to take action, be more explicit:</p>
<div data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden border border-border-300 rounded-lg my-6"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="flex"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_57uinpfdaiv6brkljb_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_17uinpfdaiv6brkljb_" class="group w-full flex items-center gap-2 p-4 text-left transparent hover:bg-bg-300 focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-accent-secondary-100 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="text-text-500 transition-transform duration-200 flex-shrink-0 group-data-[state=&#x27;open&#x27;]:rotate-90" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M181.66,133.66l-80,80a8,8,0,0,1-11.32-11.32L164.69,128,90.34,53.66a8,8,0,0,1,11.32-11.32l80,80A8,8,0,0,1,181.66,133.66Z"></path></svg><span class="font-semibold text-text-100 flex-1 font-ui">Example: Explicit instructions</span></button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_57uinpfdaiv6brkljb_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="accordion-example:-explicit-instructions" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">To make Claude more proactive about taking action by default, you can add this to your system prompt:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt for proactive action</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none

  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center justify-center"><div class="flex items-center justify-center transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" 13H12.5C12.7761 13 13 12.7761 13 12.5V4.5C13 4.22386 12.7761 4 12.5 4H4.5Z"></path></svg></div><div class="flex items-center justify-center absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>&lt;default_to_action&gt;
By default, implement changes rather than only suggesting them. If the user&#x27;s intent is unclear, infer the most useful likely action and proceed, using tools to discover any missing details instead of guessing. Try to infer the user&#x27;s intent about whether a tool call (e.g., file edit or read) is intended or not, and act accordingly.
&lt;/default_to_action&gt;</code></pre></div></div>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">On the other hand, if you want the model to be more hesitant by default, less prone to jumping straight into implementations, and only take action if requested, you can steer this behavior with a prompt like the below:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt for conservative action</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex

  shrink-0

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>&lt;do_not_act_before_instructions&gt;
Do not jump into implementatation or changes files unless clearly instructed to make changes. When the user&#x27;s intent is ambiguous, default to providing information, doing research, and providing recommendations rather than taking action. Only proceed with edits, modifications, or implementations when the user explicitly requests them.
&lt;/do_not_act_before_instructions&gt;</code></pre></div></div>

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Tool usage and triggering</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.5 is more responsive to the system prompt than previous models. If your prompts were designed to reduce undertriggering on tools or skills, Claude Opus 4.5 may now overtrigger. The fix is to dial back any aggressive language. Where you might have said &quot;CRITICAL: You MUST use this tool when...&quot;, you can use more normal prompting like &quot;Use this tool when...&quot;.</p>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="control-the-format-of-responses"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Control the format of responses</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">There are a few ways that we have found to be particularly effective in steering output formatting in Claude 4.x models:</p>
<ol class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item]">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Tell Claude what to do instead of what not to do</strong></p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Instead of: &quot;Do not use markdown in your response&quot;</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Try: &quot;Your response should be composed of smoothly flowing prose paragraphs.&quot;</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Use XML format indicators</strong></p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Try: &quot;Write the prose sections of your response in &lt;smoothly_flowing_prose_paragraphs&gt; tags.&quot;</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Match your prompt style to the desired output</strong></p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">The formatting style used in your prompt may influence Claude&#x27;s response style. If you are still experiencing steerability issues with output formatting, we recommend as best as you can matching your prompt style to your desired output style. For example, removing markdown from your prompt can reduce the volume of markdown in the output.</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Use detailed prompts for specific formatting preferences</strong></p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For more control over markdown and formatting usage, provide explicit guidance:</p>
</li>
</ol>

duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>&lt;avoid_excessive_markdown_and_bullet_points&gt;
When writing reports, documents, technical explanations, analyses, or any long-form content, write in clear, flowing prose using complete paragraphs and sentences. Use standard paragraph breaks for organization and reserve markdown primarily for `inline code`, code blocks (```...```), and simple headings (###, and ###). Avoid using **bold** and *italics*.

DO NOT use ordered lists (1. ...) or unordered lists (*) unless : a) you&#x27;re presenting truly discrete items where a list format is the best option, or b) the user explicitly requests a list or ranking

Instead of listing items with bullets or numbers, incorporate them naturally into sentences. This guidance applies especially to technical writing. Using prose instead of excessive formatting will improve user satisfaction. NEVER output a series of overly short bullet points.

Your goal is readable, flowing text that guides the reader naturally through ideas rather than fragmenting information into isolated points.
&lt;/avoid_excessive_markdown_and_bullet_points&gt;</code></pre></div></div>

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.5 models demonstrate exceptional agentic search capabilities and can find and synthesize information from multiple sources effectively. For optimal research results:</p>
<ol class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item]">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Provide clear success criteria</strong>: Define what constitutes a successful answer to your research question</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Encourage source verification</strong>: Ask Claude to verify information across multiple sources</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.5 models demonstrate significantly improved native subagent orchestration capabilities. These models can recognize when tasks would benefit from delegating work to specialized subagents and do so proactively without requiring explicit instruction.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">To take advantage of this behavior:</p>
<ol class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item]">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Ensure well-defined subagent tools</strong>: Have subagent tools available and described in tool definitions</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Let Claude orchestrate naturally</strong>: Claude will delegate appropriately without explicit instruction</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Adjust conservativeness if needed</strong>:</li>
</ol>

<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="model-self-knowledge"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">When extended thinking is disabled, Claude Opus 4.5 is particularly sensitive to the word &quot;think&quot; and its variants. We recommend replacing &quot;think&quot; with alternative words that convey similar meaning, such as &quot;consider,&quot; &quot;believe,&quot; and &quot;evaluate.&quot;</p>

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.5 models excel at creating presentations, animations, and visual documents. These models match or exceed Claude Opus 4.1 in this domain, with impressive creative flair and stronger instruction following. The models produce polished, usable output on the first try in most cases.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For best results with document creation:</p>

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.5 has improved vision capabilities compared to previous Claude models. It performs better on image processing and data extraction tasks, particularly when there are multiple images present in context. These improvements carry over to computer use, where the model can more reliably interpret screenshots and UI elements. You can also use Claude Opus 4.5 to analyze videos by breaking them up into frames.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">One technique we&#x27;ve found effective to further boost performance is to give Claude Opus 4.5 a crop tool or <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agents-and-tools/agent-skills/overview">skill</a>. We&#x27;ve seen consistent uplift on image evaluations when Claude is able to &quot;zoom&quot; in on relevant regions of an image. We&#x27;ve put together a cookbook for the crop tool <a class="inline-link" href="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-cookbooks/blob/main/multimodal/crop_tool.ipynb">here</a>.</p>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="optimize-parallel-tool-calling"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.x models excel at parallel tool execution, with Sonnet 4.5 being particularly aggressive in firing off multiple operations simultaneously. Claude 4.x models will:</p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Run multiple speculative searches during research</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Read several files at once to build context faster</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Execute bash commands in parallel (which can even bottleneck system performance)</li>
</ul>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">This behavior is easily steerable. While the model has a high success rate in parallel tool calling without prompting, you can boost this to ~100% or adjust the aggression level:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt for maximum parallel efficiency</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent

          font-base
          duration-300

opacity-0" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>&lt;use_parallel_tool_calls&gt;
If you intend to call multiple tools and there are no dependencies between the tool calls, make all of the independent tool calls in parallel. Prioritize calling tools simultaneously whenever the actions can be done in parallel rather than sequentially. For example, when reading 3 files, run 3 tool calls in parallel to read all 3 files into context at the same time. Maximize use of parallel tool calls where possible to increase speed and efficiency. However, if some tool calls depend on previous calls to inform dependent values like the parameters, do NOT call these tools in parallel and instead call them sequentially. Never use placeholders or guess missing parameters in tool calls.
&lt;/use_parallel_tool_calls&gt;</code></pre></div></div>

<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="reduce-file-creation-in-agentic-coding"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Reduce file creation in agentic coding</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.x models may sometimes create new files for testing and iteration purposes, particularly when working with code. This approach allows Claude to use files, especially python scripts, as a &#x27;temporary scratchpad&#x27; before saving its final output. Using temporary files can improve outcomes particularly for agentic coding use cases.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">If you&#x27;d prefer to minimize net new file creation, you can instruct Claude to clean up after itself:</p>

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.5 has a tendency to overengineer by creating extra files, adding unnecessary abstractions, or building in flexibility that wasn&#x27;t requested. If you&#x27;re seeing this undesired behavior, add explicit prompting to keep solutions minimal.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For example:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt to minimize overengineering</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center

  select-none

  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center justify-center"><div class="flex items-center justify-center transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12.5 3C13.3284 3 14 3.67157 14 4.5V6H15.5C16.3284 6 17 6.67157 17 7.5V15.5C17 16.3284 16.3284 17 15.5 17H7.5C6.67157 17 6 16.3284 6 15.5V14H4.5C3.67157 14 3 13.3284 3 12.5V4.5C3 3.67157 3.67157 3 4.5 3H12.5ZM14 12.5C14 13.3284 13H12.5C12.7761 13 13 12.7761 13 12.5V4.5C13 4.22386 12.7761 4 12.5 4H4.5Z"></path></svg></div><div class="flex items-center justify-center absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>Avoid over-engineering. Only make changes that are directly requested or clearly necessary. Keep solutions simple and focused.

Don&#x27;t add features, refactor code, or make &quot;improvements&quot; beyond what was asked. A bug fix doesn&#x27;t need surrounding code cleaned up. A simple feature doesn&#x27;t need extra configurability.

Don&#x27;t add error handling, fallbacks, or validation for scenarios that can&#x27;t happen. Trust internal code and framework guarantees. Only validate at system boundaries (user input, external APIs). Don&#x27;t use backwards-compatibility shims when you can just change the code.

Don&#x27;t create helpers, utilities, or abstractions for one-time operations. Don&#x27;t design for hypothetical future requirements. The right amount of complexity is the minimum needed for the current task. Reuse existing abstractions where possible and follow the DRY principle.</code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="frontend-design"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
