<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.x models, particularly Opus 4.5, excel at building complex, real-world web applications with strong frontend design. However, without guidance, models can default to generic patterns that create what users call the &quot;AI slop&quot; aesthetic. To create distinctive, creative frontends that surprise and delight:</p>
<div class="flex w-full rounded-lg p-2 px-4 gap-1 items-start text-sm border-0.5 my-6 border-border-200 bg-bg-200 callout"><div class="flex mr-2 shrink-0 pt-[1.375px] text-text-000"><div class="flex items-center justify-center" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12.5 17C12.7761 17 13 17.2239 13 17.5C13 17.7761 12.7761 18 12.5 18H7.5C7.22386 18 7 17.7761 7 17.5C7 17.2239 7.22386 17 7.5 17H12.5ZM10 2C13.3137 2 16 4.68629 16 8C16 9.73776 15.2608 11.3033 14.0811 12.3984L13.8389 12.6113C13.3268 13.0382 13 13.5753 13 14.124V15.5C13 15.7761 12.7761 16 12.5 16H7.5C7.22386 16 7 15.7761 7 15.5V14.124C6.99998 13.6438 6.7495 13.1727 6.34375 12.7764L6.16113 12.6113C4.84147 11.5115 4 9.85368 4 8C4 4.68629 6.68629 2 10 2ZM10 3C7.23858 3 5 5.23858 5 8C5 9.5443 5.69948 10.9248 6.80078 11.8428L7.03711 12.0557C7.57356 12.5787 7.99998 13.2899 8 14.124V15H9.5V11.207L7.14648 8.85352L7.08203 8.77539C6.95387 8.58131 6.97562 8.31735 7.14648 8.14648C7.31735 7.97562 7.58131 7.95387 7.77539 8.08203L7.85352 8.14648L10 10.293L12.1465 8.14648L12.2246 8.08203C12.4187 7.95387 12.6827 7.97562 12.8535 8.14648C13.0244 8.31735 13.0461 8.58131 12.918 8.77539L12.8535 8.85352L10.5 11.207V15H12V14.124C12 13.1706 12.5575 12.3776 13.1992 11.8428L13.4004 11.665C14.3848 10.7513 15 9.44786 15 8C15 5.23858 12.7614 3 10 3Z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="grow min-w-0 leading-relaxed text-text-000 [&amp;_li]:before:text-text-000/60 [&amp;_blockquote]:border-l-text-000/60 [&amp;_code]:text-text-000 [&amp;_code]:bg-text-000/10"><p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For a detailed guide on improving frontend design, see our blog post on <a class="inline-link" href="https://www.claude.com/blog/improving-frontend-design-through-skills">improving frontend design through skills</a>.</p></div></div>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Here&#x27;s a system prompt snippet you can use to encourage better frontend design:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt for frontend aesthetics</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center justify-center"><div class="flex items-center justify-center transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12.5 3C13.3284 3 14 3.67157 14 4.5V6H15.5C16.3284 6 17 6.67157 17 7.5V15.5C17 16.3284 16.3284 17 15.5 17H7.5C6.67157 17 6 16.3284 6 15.5V14H4.5C3.67157 14 3 13.3284 3 12.5V4.5C3 3.67157 3.67157 3 4.5 3H12.5ZM14 12.5C14 13.3284 13.3284 14 12.5 14H7V15.5C7 15.7761 7.22386 16 7.5 16H15.5C15.7761 16 16 15.7761 16 15.5V7.5C16 7.22386 15.7761 7 15.5 7H14V12.5ZM4.5 4C4.22386 4 4 4.22386 4 4.5V12.5C4 12.7761 4.22386 13 4.5 13H12.5C12.7761 13 13 12.7761 13 12.5V4.5C13 4.22386 12.7761 4 12.5 4H4.5Z"></path></svg></div><div class="flex items-center justify-center absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>&lt;frontend_aesthetics&gt;
You tend to converge toward generic, &quot;on distribution&quot; outputs. In frontend design, this creates what users call the &quot;AI slop&quot; aesthetic. Avoid this: make creative, distinctive frontends that surprise and delight.

Focus on:
- Typography: Choose fonts that are beautiful, unique, and interesting. Avoid generic fonts like Arial and Inter; opt instead for distinctive choices that elevate the frontend&#x27;s aesthetics.
- Color &amp; Theme: Commit to a cohesive aesthetic. Use CSS variables for consistency. Dominant colors with sharp accents outperform timid, evenly-distributed palettes. Draw from IDE themes and cultural aesthetics for inspiration.
- Motion: Use animations for effects and micro-interactions. Prioritize CSS-only solutions for HTML. Use Motion library for React when available. Focus on high-impact moments: one well-orchestrated page load with staggered reveals (animation-delay) creates more delight than scattered micro-interactions.
- Backgrounds: Create atmosphere and depth rather than defaulting to solid colors. Layer CSS gradients, use geometric patterns, or add contextual effects that match the overall aesthetic.

Avoid generic AI-generated aesthetics:
- Overused font families (Inter, Roboto, Arial, system fonts)
- ClichÃ©d color schemes (particularly purple gradients on white backgrounds)
- Predictable layouts and component patterns
- Cookie-cutter design that lacks context-specific character

Interpret creatively and make unexpected choices that feel genuinely designed for the context. Vary between light and dark themes, different fonts, different aesthetics. You still tend to converge on common choices (Space Grotesk, for example) across generations. Avoid this: it is critical that you think outside the box!
&lt;/frontend_aesthetics&gt;</code></pre></div></div>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">You can also refer to the full skill <a class="inline-link" href="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/blob/main/plugins/frontend-design/skills/frontend-design/SKILL.md">here</a>.</p>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="avoid-focusing-on-passing-tests-and-hard-coding"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Avoid focusing on passing tests and hard-coding</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.x models can sometimes focus too heavily on making tests pass at the expense of more general solutions, or may use workarounds like helper scripts for complex refactoring instead of using standard tools directly. To prevent this behavior and ensure robust, generalizable solutions:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex

  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent

          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center 13H12.5C12.7761 13 13 12.7761 13 12.5V4.5C13 4.22386 12.7761 4 12.5 4H4.5Z"></path></svg></div><div class="flex items-center justify-center absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>Please write a high-quality, general-purpose solution using the standard tools available. Do not create helper scripts or workarounds to accomplish the task more efficiently. Implement a solution that works correctly for all valid inputs, not just the test cases. Do not hard-code values or create solutions that only work for specific test inputs. Instead, implement the actual logic that solves the problem generally.

Focus on understanding the problem requirements and implementing the correct algorithm. Tests are there to verify correctness, not to define the solution. Provide a principled implementation that follows best practices and software design principles.

If the task is unreasonable or infeasible, or if any of the tests are incorrect, please inform me rather than working around them. The solution should be robust, maintainable, and extendable.</code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="encouraging-code-exploration"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.5 is highly capable but can be overly conservative when exploring code. If you notice the model proposing solutions without looking at the code or making assumptions about code it hasn&#x27;t read, the best solution is to add explicit instructions to the prompt. Claude Opus 4.5 is our most steerable model to date and responds reliably to direct guidance.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For example:</p>

  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent

          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center Do not speculate about code you have not inspected. If the user references a specific file/path, you MUST open and inspect it before explaining or proposing fixes.           ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Minimizing hallucinations in agentic coding</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Claude 4.x models are less prone to hallucinations and give more accurate, grounded, intelligent answers based on the code. To encourage this behavior even more and minimize hallucinations:</p>
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt</div><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 Never speculate about code you have not opened. If the user references a specific file, you MUST read the file before answering. Make sure to investigate and read relevant files BEFORE answering questions about the codebase. Never make any claims about code before investigating unless you are certain of the correct answer - give grounded and hallucination-free answers.
&lt;/investigate_before_answering&gt;</code></pre></div></div>

          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Migration considerations</div></div></h2>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">When migrating to Claude 4.5 models:</p>
<ol class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item]">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Be specific about desired behavior</strong>: Consider describing exactly what you&#x27;d like to see in the output.</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Frame your instructions with modifiers</strong>: Adding modifiers that encourage Claude to increase the quality and detail of its output can help better shape Claude&#x27;s performance. For example, instead of &quot;Create an analytics dashboard&quot;, use &quot;Create an analytics dashboard. Include as many relevant features and interactions as possible. Go beyond the basics to create a fully-featured implementation.&quot;</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Request specific features explicitly</strong>: Animations and interactive elements should be requested explicitly when desired.</p>
</li>

Prioritize calling tools simultaneously whenever the actions can be done in parallel rather than sequentially. For example, when reading 3 files, run 3 tool calls in parallel to read all 3 files into context at the same time. Maximize use of parallel tool calls where possible to increase speed and efficiency. However, if some tool calls depend on previous calls to inform dependent values like the parameters, do NOT call these tools in parallel and instead call them sequentially. Never use placeholders or guess missing parameters in tool calls.\\n\u003c/use_parallel_tool_calls\u003e\",\"label\":\"Sample prompt for maximum parallel efficiency\"}]\n"])</script><script nonce="seW1B2dtMQYGJ1aIte9hmw==">self.__next_f.push([1,"6e:[\"$\",\"$L26\",null,{\"language\":\"text\",\"code\":\"Execute operations sequentially with brief pauses between each step to ensure stability.\",\"label\":\"Sample prompt to reduce parallel execution\"}]\n6f:[\"$\",\"h3\",null,{\"className\":\"text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"$L24\",null,{\"slug\":\"reduce-file-creation-in-agentic-coding\",\"className\":\"pt-6 pb-2\",\"children\":\"Reduce file creation in agentic coding\"}]}]\n70:[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"className\":\"mb-4 last:mb-0\",\"children\":\"Claude 4.x models may sometimes create new files for testing and iteration purposes, particularly when working with code. Only make changes that are directly requested or clearly necessary. Keep solutions simple and focused.\\n\\nDon't add features, refactor code, or make \\\"improvements\\\" beyond what was asked. A bug fix doesn't need surrounding code cleaned up. A simple feature doesn't need extra configurability.\\n\\nDon't add error handling, fallbacks, or validation for scenarios that can't happen. Avoid this: make creative, distinctive frontends that surprise and delight.\n\nFocus on:\n- Typography: Choose fonts that are beautiful, unique, and interesting. Avoid generic fonts like Arial and Inter; opt instead for distinctive choices that elevate the frontend's aesthetics.\n- Color \u0026 Theme: Commit to a cohesive aesthetic. Use CSS variables for consistency. Dominant colors with sharp accents outperform timid, evenly-distributed palettes. Draw from IDE themes and cultural aesthetics for inspiration.\n- Motion: Use animations for effects and micro-interactions. Prioritize CSS-only solutions for HTML. Use Motion library for React when available. Focus on high-impact moments: one well-orchestrated page load with staggered reveals (animation-delay) creates more delight than scattered micro-interactions.\n- Backgrounds: Create atmosphere and depth rather than defaulting to solid colors.
